It endorsed the principle of removing most copyright and licensing barriers in order to accelerate scientific progress and broaden readership. (\u003Ca href=\\\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.budapestopenaccessinitiative.org\\\"\u003Ehttp:\u002F\u002Fwww.budapestopenaccessinitiative.org\u003C\u002Fa\u003E)\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\\n\\n\u003Cp\u003EAligning with these emerging principles, IntechOpen&rsquo;s co-founders, at the time active researchers in robotics, recognized the necessity of a more open model. Inspired by this global shift in thinking, they founded the company with the goal of creating a publishing environment &quot;for scientists, by scientists,&quot; where research could be shared freely to maximize its contribution to scientific advancement.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\\n\\n\u003Cp\u003EBuilding on these foundations,&nbsp;we are committed to working with organisations and people who care about scientific discovery, putting the academic needs of the scientific community first, and providing an open access environment where scientists can maximise their contribution to scientific advancement. By opening up access to the world&rsquo;s scientific research articles and book chapters, we aim to facilitate greater opportunities for collaboration, scientific discovery and progress. We subscribe wholeheartedly to the open access definition:\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\\n\\n\u003Cp\u003E&ldquo;By &ldquo;open access&rdquo; to [peer-reviewed research literature], we mean its free availability on the public internet, permitting any users to read, download, copy, distribute, print, search, or link to the full texts of these articles, crawl them for indexing, pass them as data to software, or use them for any other lawful purpose, without financial, legal, or technical barriers other than those inseparable from gaining access to the internet itself. The only constraint on reproduction and distribution, and the only role for copyright in this domain, should be to give authors control over the integrity of their work and the right to be properly acknowledged and cited&rdquo; (\u003Ca href=\\\"http:\u002F\u002Fwww.budapestopenaccessinitiative.org\\\"\u003Ehttp:\u002F\u002Fwww.budapestopenaccessinitiative.org\u003C\u002Fa\u003E)\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\\n\\n\u003Ch2\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EOpen Access Standards and Principles Followed by IntechOpen\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fh2\u003E\\n\\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EOASPA \u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\\n\\n\u003Cp\u003EWe have been a member of OASPA since 2019, meet all membership criteria, and follow their Code of Conduct.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\\n\\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003ELicenses\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\\n\\n\u003Cp\u003EBook chapters published in edited volumes, and all journal articles, are distributed under the Creative Commons 4.0 International License (CC BY 4.0). There is no copyright transfer to the publisher, and the Authors retain exclusive copyright to their work. All Monographs\u002FCompacts are distributed under the Creative Commons Attribution-NonCommercial 4.0 International License (CC BY-NC 4.0).&nbsp;\u003Ca href=\\\"copyright-policy\\\"\u003ERead more&nbsp;\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\\n\\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EPeer Review Policy\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\\n\\n\u003Cp\u003EAll scientific works are peer reviewed prior to publishing to ensure unbiased and expert evaluation of scholarly work.&nbsp;\u003Ca href=\\\"peer-reviewing\\\"\u003ERead more\u003C\u002Fa\u003E.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\\n\\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EResearch Integrity and Publication Ethics\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\\n\\n\u003Cp\u003EWe establish and maintain clear editorial guidelines and robust policies designed to prevent misconduct and promote ethical publishing practices. We utilise technological tools to detect issues early in the publishing process and address post-publication concerns through systematic checks, issuing corrections or retractions where fraud or misconduct is confirmed. Transparency is prioritised through open data, enhancing trust and reproducibility. Finally, we foster a culture of committment to research integrity and publication ethics, across the research and publishing process. \u003Ca href=\\\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.intechopen.com\u002Fpage\u002Feditorial-policies\\\"\u003ERead more.\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\\n\\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EAccessibility\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\\n\\n\u003Cp\u003EOur commitment to accessibility ensures that all readers, including those with disabilities, can access, read, and interact with content without barriers (HTML and PDF formats). This commitment reflects a broader goal of equity, inclusion, and compliance with global standards.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\\n\\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EOA Publishing Fees\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\\n\\n\u003Cp\u003EWe are gold open access publisher. The publishing model employed by IntechOpen eliminates subscription charges and pay-per-view fees, enabling readers to access research at no cost. In order to sustain operations and keep our publications freely accessible, we levy an open access publishing fee for manuscripts, which helps us cover the costs of editorial work and the production of books.&nbsp;\u003Ca href=\\\"\u002Fpage\u002FOA-publishing-fees\\\"\u003ERead more\u003C\u002Fa\u003E.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\\n\\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EDigital Archiving Policy\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\\n\\n\u003Cp\u003EWe are committed to ensuring the long-term preservation and availability of all scholarly research we publish. We employ various methods to fulfil our commitments to the scientific community. Our publications are preserved by the Croatian National Library (for publications prior to April 18, 2018) and the British Library (for publications published after April 18, 2018), as well as in the CLOCKSS archive, which preserves our entire catalogue.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\\n\\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EDOAB\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\\n\\n\u003Cp\u003EThe Directory of Open Access Books (DOAB) is a key platform promoting research by providing a searchable database of peer-reviewed, academic open access books from reputable publishers. Our full catalogue&nbsp; is available in the DOAB.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\\n\\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EOAI-PMH\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\\n\\n\u003Cp\u003EAs a firm believer in the wider dissemination of knowledge, we have supported the Open Access Initiative Protocol for Metadata Harvesting (OAI-PMH Version 2.0) since 2012.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\\n\\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EAccess Policy\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\\n\\n\u003Cp\u003EView more about our Access Policy \u003Ca href=\\\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.intechopen.com\u002Fpage\u002Faccess-policy\\\"\u003Ehere.\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\\n\\n\u003Ch2\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EOpen Science\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fh2\u003E\\n\\n\u003Cp\u003EOpen science is transparent and accessible knowledge that is shared and developed through collaborative networks.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\\n\\n\u003Cp\u003EOpen science is about increased rigour, accountability, and reproducibility in research. It is based on the principles of inclusion, fairness, equity, and sharing and ultimately seeks to change the way research is done, who is involved, and how it is valued. It aims to make research more open to participation, review\u002Frefutation, improvement, and (re)use so that the world can benefit from it.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\\n\\n\u003Cp\u003EOpen science refers to conducting traditional science with increased transparency at various stages, such as openly sharing code and data. It implies a growing set of practices - within different disciplines - aiming at:\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\\n\\n\u003Cul\u003E\\n\\t\u003Cli\u003EPromoting open and publicly accessible education tools\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\\n\\t\u003Cli\u003ETransparency in experimental methodology, observation, and collection of data\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\\n\\t\u003Cli\u003EReproducible research data and re-analysis\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\\n\\t\u003Cli\u003EPublic availability and re-usability of scientific data\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\\n\\t\u003Cli\u003EPublic accessibility and transparency of scientific communication\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\\n\\t\u003Cli\u003ETransparent peer-review and publishing practices\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\\n\\t\u003Cli\u003EUsing web-based tools to facilitate scientific collaboration\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\\n\\t\u003Cli\u003ESupporting exchange of knowledge and research materials between disciplines\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\\n\\t\u003Cli\u003ESupporting exchange of knowledge and research materials between scientific communities and industry.\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\\n\u003C\u002Ful\u003E\\n\\n\u003Cp\u003EWe aim at improving the quality and availability of scholarly communication by promoting and practicing:\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\\n\\n\u003Cul\u003E\\n\\t\u003Cli\u003EOpen Access\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\\n\\t\u003Cli\u003EOpen Data\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\\n\\t\u003Cli\u003EOpen Metrics and Impact\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\\n\\t\u003Cli\u003EOpen Source\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\\n\u003C\u002Ful\u003E\\n\\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EFigshare\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\\n\\n\u003Cp\u003EWe have a partnership with Figshare and an available integration between IntechOpen Journals&#39; data and Figshare&rsquo;s repository infrastructure. We&nbsp;embrace&nbsp;opportunities to collaborate with partners who share our values. Open data and transparency in research are core to open science.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\\n\\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EOpen Science Hub\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\\n\\n\u003Cp\u003EIn our commitment to open science, we have created a dedicated hub featuring resources, videos, webinars, and useful materials for learning about and getting involved in transparent, open, and accessible research. Inspired by this global shift in thinking, they founded the company with the goal of creating a publishing environment &quot;for scientists, by scientists,&quot; where research could be shared freely to maximize its contribution to scientific advancement.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\n\u003Cp\u003EBuilding on these foundations,&nbsp;we are committed to working with organisations and people who care about scientific discovery, putting the academic needs of the scientific community first, and providing an open access environment where scientists can maximise their contribution to scientific advancement. By opening up access to the world&rsquo;s scientific research articles and book chapters, we aim to facilitate greater opportunities for collaboration, scientific discovery and progress. We subscribe wholeheartedly to the open access definition:\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\n\u003Cp\u003E&ldquo;By &ldquo;open access&rdquo; to [peer-reviewed research literature], we mean its free availability on the public internet, permitting any users to read, download, copy, distribute, print, search, or link to the full texts of these articles, crawl them for indexing, pass them as data to software, or use them for any other lawful purpose, without financial, legal, or technical barriers other than those inseparable from gaining access to the internet itself. We utilise technological tools to detect issues early in the publishing process and address post-publication concerns through systematic checks, issuing corrections or retractions where fraud or misconduct is confirmed. Transparency is prioritised through open data, enhancing trust and reproducibility. Finally, we foster a culture of committment to research integrity and publication ethics, across the research and publishing process. \u003Ca href=\"https:\u002F\u002Fwww.intechopen.com\u002Fpage\u002Feditorial-policies\"\u003ERead more.\u003C\u002Fa\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EAccessibility\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\n\u003Cp\u003EOur commitment to accessibility ensures that all readers, including those with disabilities, can access, read, and interact with content without barriers (HTML and PDF formats). We employ various methods to fulfil our commitments to the scientific community. Our publications are preserved by the Croatian National Library (for publications prior to April 18, 2018) and the British Library (for publications published after April 18, 2018), as well as in the CLOCKSS archive, which preserves our entire catalogue.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EDOAB\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\n\u003Cp\u003EThe Directory of Open Access Books (DOAB) is a key platform promoting research by providing a searchable database of peer-reviewed, academic open access books from reputable publishers. It is based on the principles of inclusion, fairness, equity, and sharing and ultimately seeks to change the way research is done, who is involved, and how it is valued. It aims to make research more open to participation, review\u002Frefutation, improvement, and (re)use so that the world can benefit from it.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\n\u003Cp\u003EOpen science refers to conducting traditional science with increased transparency at various stages, such as openly sharing code and data. It implies a growing set of practices - within different disciplines - aiming at:\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\n\u003Cul\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003EPromoting open and publicly accessible education tools\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003ETransparency in experimental methodology, observation, and collection of data\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003EReproducible research data and re-analysis\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003EPublic availability and re-usability of scientific data\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003EPublic accessibility and transparency of scientific communication\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003ETransparent peer-review and publishing practices\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003EUsing web-based tools to facilitate scientific collaboration\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003ESupporting exchange of knowledge and research materials between disciplines\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003ESupporting exchange of knowledge and research materials between scientific communities and industry.\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ful\u003E\n\n\u003Cp\u003EWe aim at improving the quality and availability of scholarly communication by promoting and practicing:\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\n\u003Cul\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003EOpen Access\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003EOpen Data\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003EOpen Metrics and Impact\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\t\u003Cli\u003EOpen Source\u003C\u002Fli\u003E\n\u003C\u002Ful\u003E\n\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EFigshare\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\n\u003Cp\u003EWe have a partnership with Figshare and an available integration between IntechOpen Journals&#39; data and Figshare&rsquo;s repository infrastructure. We&nbsp;embrace&nbsp;opportunities to collaborate with partners who share our values. Open data and transparency in research are core to open science.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\n\u003Cp\u003E\u003Cstrong\u003EOpen Science Hub\u003C\u002Fstrong\u003E\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\n\u003Cp\u003EIn our commitment to open science, we have created a dedicated hub featuring resources, videos, webinars, and useful materials for learning about and getting involved in transparent, open, and accessible research. Recent attention has focused on how LLMs have the potential to reduce faculty time and effort in creating assessment items, but prior studies predominantly focus on a single LLM model (ChatGPT) and usually do not employ exemplars. We investigated the capabilities of three GPT and five Claude LLM models in creating medical board-style assessment items with two-shot biochemistry exemplars. The generated questions were evaluated by biomedical science educators in their respective fields for their accuracy, educational value, and overall quality. The findings indicate a notable potential of these LLMs in medical education, with the OpenAI ChatGPTs and Claude-V2 AIs demonstrating an ability to produce particularly high-quality assessment items. However, exemplars for each specific discipline may be required to increase the quality of the questions, as anatomy questions performed more poorly. Automated daily creation of exam banks with specified percentages across question categories was also tested, showing initial accuracy but degrading over time. In addition, we developed a GPT-4o-based interactive bot to build medical assessment items, called medStudent QandA, that is free and accessible to all OpenAI account holders (including free-tier users at the time of publication). Yet alongside these opportunities arise significant risks related to equity, privacy, transparency, and student agency. This chapter advances the framework of bidirectional human&ndash;AI alignment in education, arguing that trustworthy learning environments require more than embedding human values into AI systems. Instead, alignment must be understood as a dynamic, reciprocal process in which AI systems are designed to reflect shared educational values, while educators and learners develop the literacy and agency to interpret, critique, and guide AI technologies.We first clarify what must be aligned&mdash;core ethical principles, substantive educational goals, and human&ndash;AI interaction norms. We then outline three complementary pathways for achieving alignment: (1) human-centered and value-sensitive technical design, (2) ethical, legal, and governance frameworks, and (3) continuous evaluation and adaptive feedback mechanisms. The chapter further traces AI&rsquo;s evolving role from support tool to collaborative partner and interactive tutor, examining its impact on teacher practice, student autonomy, assessment, and educational governance.By reframing AI adoption as an ongoing process of mutual adaptation rather than one-way control, this chapter offers actionable recommendations for policymakers, developers, institutions, and educators. Conventional testing methods often struggle to address the challenge of complexity and non-determinism in deep learning models. Metamorphic testing employs pre-defined metamorphic&ensp;relations to derive expected behavior from transformed inputs, enabling validation without explicit ground truth. Mutation-based testing, on the other hand, injects deliberate faults into the model or dataset to assess system robustness and uncover latent defects. This integrated approach enhances test coverage and supports the generation of diverse, adversarial, and edge-case data. By leveraging metamorphic relations and systematically injecting mutations into models and data, this approach addresses the oracle problem and uncovers hidden inconsistencies. The chapter highlights how these methods contribute to robust validation processes, ensuring integrity, reliability, and transparency in AI-driven applications. This aligns with the broader scope of promoting best practices for data quality, integrity, and assurance in intelligent systems.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\n","isPublished":false,"isOnlineFirst":true,"isDeactivated":null,"isDeactivated2":0,"deactCorrection":null,"book":{"id":"1004801","title":"Data Quality Matters - Best Practices for Integrity and Assurance","coverURL":"https:\u002F\u002Fintech-files.s3.amazonaws.com\u002Fa04Tc00000ClgZiIAJ\u002F0016705_TrikoderCover%20%282024-12-18%2009%3A41%3A37%29.jpg","isOpenForSubmission":false,"isPublished":false},"signatures":"Radziah Mohamad, Junhan Li, Tan Ser Xuen, Johanna Ahmad\r\nand Alif Ridzuan Khairuddin"},{"id":"1235771","title":"Trustworthiness Assurance for Model Updates in Federated Learning","slug":null,"totalDownloads":0,"totalDimensionsCites":null,"doi":"10.5772\u002Fintechopen.1013666","abstract":"\n\n\u003Cp\u003ETraining accurate Machine Learning (ML) models requires access to large volumes of data, often personal or confidential, raising significant privacy concerns under certain rules and regulations. Traditional protection methods, such as data encryption, are effective in protecting data content but hinder ML model training by preventing access to the underlying data. This challenge has led to the development of privacy-preserving ML techniques, i.e., the Federated Learning (FL), where the centralized training process in conventional approaches has been outsourced to multiple and distributed nodes, each with its own dataset. Although researchers, developers, and innovators enjoy the advantages of such a concept in terms of privacy protection, reduced cost (i.e., equipment, computational cost), improved model customization (personalization and generalization), and scalability, the distributed and uncontrolled nature of nodes in FL schemes can introduce some anomalies during the local training process that may have a negative effect on the trustworthiness of model updates. These anomalies may be intentional, such as adversarial model poisoning by malicious clients, or unintentional, resulting from data heterogeneity, communication failures, or resource constraints. Both types of anomalies can severely degrade the performance and trustworthiness of the global model. This chapter addresses the challenge of detecting and mitigating such abnormalities by proposing MultiTrust-FL: a multi-layered trustworthiness assurance framework for FL for detecting anomalies and evaluating the reputation of clients, while providing defense mechanisms for robust and secure aggregation, secure transmission, and backdoor attack detection. Finally, we present an empirical validation to show the effectiveness of MultiTrust-FL using different simulation scenarios.\u003C\u002Fp\u003E\n\n","isPublished":false,"isOnlineFirst":true,"isDeactivated":null,"isDeactivated2":0,"deactCorrection":null,"book":{"id":"1004801","title":"Data Quality Matters - Best Practices for Integrity and Assurance","coverURL":"https:\u002F\u002Fintech-files.s3.amazonaws.com\u002Fa04Tc00000ClgZiIAJ\u002F0016705_TrikoderCover%20%282024-12-18%2009%3A41%3A37%29.jpg","isOpenForSubmission":false,"isPublished":false},"signatures":"Orhan Ermis, Djamel Khadraoui"},{"id":"1232922","title":"Immersive Worlds for Metalearning: Revolutionizing Scientific Understanding in the Metaverse","slug":null,"totalDownloads":6,"totalDimensionsCites":null,"doi":"10.5772\u002Fintechopen.1012652","abstract":"\n\n\u003Cp\u003EThis chapter explores the transformative potential of incorporating the metaverse, artificial intelligence (AI), and metaintelligence into science education. Usha has been a keynote speaker as well as an invited speaker at national and international conferences, seminars and workshops. Her teaching experience includes teaching in Asian countries. She has advised Austrade, APEC, national, state and local governments. She serves as a reviewer and a member of the scientific committee for national and international refereed journals and refereed conferences. She is on the editorial board for refereed journals and has worked on Special Issues. Usha has served and continues to serve on the Boards of several not-for-profit organisations and she has also served as panel judge for a number of awards including the Premiers Sustainability Award in Victoria and the International Green Gown Awards. Usha has published over 100 publications, including research and consulting reports. Her publications cover a wide range of scientific and technical research publications that include edited books, book chapters, refereed journals, refereed conference papers and reports for local, state and federal government clients. She has also produced podcasts for various organisations and participated in media interviews. She has received state, national and international funding worth over USD $25 million. Usha has been awarded the Quarterly Franklin Membership by London Journals Press (UK). Her biography has been included in the Marquis Who's Who in the World® 2018, 2016 (33rd Edition), along with approximately 55,000 of the most accomplished men and women from around the world, including luminaries as U.N. Secretary-General Ban Ki-moon. Cell\u002FModule Parameters Identification","slug":"static-and-dynamic-photovoltaic-cell-module-parameters-identification","doi":"10.5772\u002Fintechopen.89449","abstract":"The accurate parameters extraction is an important step to obtain a robust PV outputs forecasting for static or dynamic modes. For these aims, several approaches have been proposed for photovoltaic (PV) cell modeling including electrical circuit-based model, empirical models, and non-parametrical models. Moreover, numerous parameter extraction methods have been introduced in the literature depending on the proposed model and the operating mode. These methods can be classified into two main approaches including automatic numerical and analytical approaches. These approaches are commonly applied in the static mode, whereas they can be employed for dynamic parameters extraction. In this chapter, as a first stage, the static parameters extraction for both single and double diodes models is exposed wherein Genetic Algorithm and outdoor measurements are considered for fixed irradiation and temperature. In the second stage, a dynamic parameters extraction is carried out using Levenberg-Marquardt algorithm, where 1 day profile outdoor measurement is considered. After that, the robustness of the proposed approaches is evaluated and the parameters obtained by the static method and that given by the dynamic technique are compared. The test is carried out using 3 days with different weather conditions profiles. The obtained results show that the parameters extraction by dynamic techniques gives satisfactory performances in terms of agreement with the real data.","signatures":"Sid-Ali Blaifi and Bilal Taghezouit","isPublished":true,"isOnlineFirst":false,"isDeactivated":0,"isDeactivated2":0,"deactCorrection":null,"totalDownloads":1247,"totalCites":2,"totalDimensionsCites":2,"totalCrossrefCites":0,"hasAltmetrics":0,"totalAltmetricsMentions":0,"authors":[{"id":"302376","institution":null},{"id":"310085","institution":{"id":"25160"}}],"book":{"id":"9425","title":"Advanced Statistical Modeling, Forecasting, and Fault Detection in Renewable Energy Systems","isPublished":true}}],"mostCitedChapters":[{"id":"69367","title":"Static and Dynamic Photovoltaic Cell\u002FModule Parameters Identification","slug":"static-and-dynamic-photovoltaic-cell-module-parameters-identification","doi":"10.5772\u002Fintechopen.89449","abstract":"The accurate parameters extraction is an important step to obtain a robust PV outputs forecasting for static or dynamic modes.
